\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{queue_8c_source_l00055}00055 \textcolor{comment}{/* When the Queue\_t structure is used to represent a base queue its pcHead and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{queue_8c_source_l00056}00056 \textcolor{comment}{pcTail members are used as pointers into the queue storage area.  When the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{queue_8c_source_l00057}00057 \textcolor{comment}{Queue\_t structure is used to represent a mutex pcHead and pcTail pointers are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{queue_8c_source_l00058}00058 \textcolor{comment}{not necessary, and the pcHead pointer is set to NULL to indicate that the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{queue_8c_source_l00059}00059 \textcolor{comment}{structure instead holds a pointer to the mutex holder (if any).  Map alternative}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{queue_8c_source_l00060}00060 \textcolor{comment}{names to the pcHead and structure member to ensure the readability of the code}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{queue_8c_source_l00061}00061 \textcolor{comment}{is maintained.  The QueuePointers\_t and SemaphoreData\_t types are used to form}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{queue_8c_source_l00062}00062 \textcolor{comment}{a union as their usage is mutually exclusive dependent on what the queue is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{queue_8c_source_l00063}00063 \textcolor{comment}{being used for. */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{queue_8c_source_l00168}00168 \textcolor{comment}{ * prevent an ISR from adding or removing items to the queue, but does prevent}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{queue_8c_source_l00388}00388         \textcolor{comment}{/* Allocate the queue and storage area.  Justification for MISRA}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{queue_8c_source_l00389}00389 \textcolor{comment}{        deviation as follows:  pvPortMalloc() always ensures returned memory}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{queue_8c_source_l00390}00390 \textcolor{comment}{        blocks are aligned per the requirements of the MCU stack.  In this case}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{queue_8c_source_l00391}00391 \textcolor{comment}{        pvPortMalloc() must return a pointer that is guaranteed to meet the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{queue_8c_source_l00392}00392 \textcolor{comment}{        alignment requirements of the Queue\_t structure -\/ which in this case}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{queue_8c_source_l00393}00393 \textcolor{comment}{        is an int8\_t *.  Therefore, whenever the stack alignment requirements}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{queue_8c_source_l00394}00394 \textcolor{comment}{        are greater than or equal to the pointer to char requirements the cast}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{queue_8c_source_l00395}00395 \textcolor{comment}{        is safe.  In other cases alignment requirements are not strict (one or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{queue_8c_source_l00396}00396 \textcolor{comment}{        two bytes). */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{queue_8c_source_l00397}00397         pxNewQueue = ( \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_queue_definition}{Queue\_t}} * ) \mbox{\hyperlink{heap__3_8c_ac56bcb7515f081a5b3df83935499fa4a}{pvPortMalloc}}( \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}( \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_queue_definition}{Queue\_t}} ) + xQueueSizeInBytes ); \textcolor{comment}{/*lint !e9087 !e9079 see comment above. */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{queue_8c_source_l00967}00967     \textcolor{comment}{/* RTOS ports that support interrupt nesting have the concept of a maximum}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{queue_8c_source_l00968}00968 \textcolor{comment}{    system call (or maximum API call) interrupt priority.  Interrupts that are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{queue_8c_source_l00969}00969 \textcolor{comment}{    above the maximum system call priority are kept permanently enabled, even}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{queue_8c_source_l00970}00970 \textcolor{comment}{    when the RTOS kernel is in a critical section, but cannot make any calls to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{queue_8c_source_l00971}00971 \textcolor{comment}{    FreeRTOS API functions.  If configASSERT() is defined in FreeRTOSConfig.h}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{queue_8c_source_l00972}00972 \textcolor{comment}{    then portASSERT\_IF\_INTERRUPT\_PRIORITY\_INVALID() will result in an assertion}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{queue_8c_source_l00973}00973 \textcolor{comment}{    failure if a FreeRTOS API function is called from an interrupt that has been}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{queue_8c_source_l00974}00974 \textcolor{comment}{    assigned a priority above the configured maximum system call priority.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{queue_8c_source_l00975}00975 \textcolor{comment}{    Only FreeRTOS functions that end in FromISR can be called from interrupts}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{queue_8c_source_l00976}00976 \textcolor{comment}{    that have been assigned a priority at or (logically) below the maximum}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{queue_8c_source_l00977}00977 \textcolor{comment}{    system call interrupt priority.  FreeRTOS maintains a separate interrupt}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{queue_8c_source_l00978}00978 \textcolor{comment}{    safe API to ensure interrupt entry is as fast and as simple as possible.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{queue_8c_source_l00979}00979 \textcolor{comment}{    More information (albeit Cortex-\/M specific) is provided on the following}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{queue_8c_source_l01131}01131     \textcolor{comment}{/* RTOS ports that support interrupt nesting have the concept of a maximum}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{queue_8c_source_l01132}01132 \textcolor{comment}{    system call (or maximum API call) interrupt priority.  Interrupts that are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{queue_8c_source_l01133}01133 \textcolor{comment}{    above the maximum system call priority are kept permanently enabled, even}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{queue_8c_source_l01134}01134 \textcolor{comment}{    when the RTOS kernel is in a critical section, but cannot make any calls to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{queue_8c_source_l01135}01135 \textcolor{comment}{    FreeRTOS API functions.  If configASSERT() is defined in FreeRTOSConfig.h}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{queue_8c_source_l01136}01136 \textcolor{comment}{    then portASSERT\_IF\_INTERRUPT\_PRIORITY\_INVALID() will result in an assertion}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{queue_8c_source_l01137}01137 \textcolor{comment}{    failure if a FreeRTOS API function is called from an interrupt that has been}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{queue_8c_source_l01138}01138 \textcolor{comment}{    assigned a priority above the configured maximum system call priority.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{queue_8c_source_l01139}01139 \textcolor{comment}{    Only FreeRTOS functions that end in FromISR can be called from interrupts}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{queue_8c_source_l01140}01140 \textcolor{comment}{    that have been assigned a priority at or (logically) below the maximum}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{queue_8c_source_l01141}01141 \textcolor{comment}{    system call interrupt priority.  FreeRTOS maintains a separate interrupt}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{queue_8c_source_l01142}01142 \textcolor{comment}{    safe API to ensure interrupt entry is as fast and as simple as possible.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{queue_8c_source_l01143}01143 \textcolor{comment}{    More information (albeit Cortex-\/M specific) is provided on the following}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{queue_8c_source_l01144}01144 \textcolor{comment}{    link: http://www.freertos.org/RTOS-\/Cortex-\/M3-\/M4.html */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{queue_8c_source_l01792}01792     \textcolor{comment}{/* RTOS ports that support interrupt nesting have the concept of a maximum}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{queue_8c_source_l01793}01793 \textcolor{comment}{    system call (or maximum API call) interrupt priority.  Interrupts that are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{queue_8c_source_l01794}01794 \textcolor{comment}{    above the maximum system call priority are kept permanently enabled, even}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{queue_8c_source_l02750}02750 \textcolor{comment}{        time a yield will be performed.  If an item is added to the queue while}}
